SHIS PA BRJOD, ,ZHAR BA SGUR PO NAD PA MI'U THUNG RNAMS KYIS,

NI NGES PAR ZHUGS GNAS PHRA RNAMS LAS, ,LHA YI RJES 'GRO RGYAL
MTSAN BZHIN DU RAB TU BTUD, ,DE NAS GZHON NU NGES PAR GSHEGS ZHES

'DOD PAS LDING KHANG SHOD DU SONG BAR GYUR, ,YON TAN SKA RAGS
BRUL ZHING GEGS BYAS DE RNAMS NI, ,GNYID LOG RAB TU SAD PAS LTA

BYED 'KHRUGS PA RNAMS, ,GNAS LUGS GTAM GYIS RNAM PAR BRGYAN RNAMS
RNAM GZHAG STE, ,YA MTSAN GYUR PAS DOGS MED PAR NI YONGS SU SONG,

KHYIM GYI

BYA YI TSOGS RNAMS NI, ,PHAN TSUN SHUGS RNAMS LAS KYANG YANG DAG
KUN NAS GTOR, ,GANG ZHIG 'DIR NI YAN LAG RAB MCHOG MA RNAMS NI,

'DZIN RNAMS RGYAS SHING SKYED SMAD SHING RTA NI, ,YANGS PA RNAMS
KYIS LCI BA NYID PHYIR

NYID DU MNYAM STE 'DI LAS NGAL BA 'DI, ,DE PHYIR SPUN GYI TSOGS
NI 'DUS NAS

'ONGS PA STE, ,BLA MA'I GDUNG RNAMS MCHOD PA LA NI BYA BA GCIG
,JI LTAR CHOS KYI CHO GA LA NI SER SNA NYID, ,NOR RNAMS LA NI SER
SNA DE LTAR SKYON MA YIN, ,SER SNA SMRA BA NGES PA NYID DU SKYON
YIN ZHING, ,SKYON NI CHOS KYI DGRA BOR GYUR PA NYID YIN NO, ,GAL
TE MI SBYIN PAR NI KHYED

@101B RNAMS KYIS NGAS NA, ,RDZONG NAS 'THON NAS 'GRON PO RNAMS LA
BSNYEN PAR MDZOD, ,GANG RNAMS KYIS STOBS MNGA' RNAMS MA YIN SGO
GLEGS RNAMS, ,DE RNAMS RIGS SU SKYES PA'I RGYAL RIGS MA YIN NO,
,BYAMS PA DANG NI GZI BRJID STON PAR BYED BZHIN DU, ,MI DBANG
RNAMS

KYIS KHYED CAG RNAMS LA DE SKAD SMRAS, ,BDAG GI SMRA 'DOD GANG
YANG RANG GIS RTOGS NAS SU, ,DGA' LAS BDAG GI DE NI KHYED CAG
RNAMS KYIS NYON, ,'GA' ZHIG RTZOD PA DGE BA MA YIN CHOS MIN TE,
,RNAM PAR 'GRAS PAR MA 'GRO ZHI BA BSNYEN PAR MDZOD, ,THUB PA DES
NI BZOD

PA RAB TU BSNGAGS PA STE, ,GANG GIS GUS PAS ME NI KUN NAS 'PHEL
BAR 'GYUR, ,NOR DANG 'DOD PA DAG GI GCIG GI CHED DU NI, ,RNAM PAR
RTZOD PA TSUL NI NYE BAR 'GYUR BA STE, ,CHOS KYI CHED DU SLAR
YANG 'PHAGS PAR GYUR PA NI, ,ZHI BA DANG NI DGRA BO RNAM PAR
RTZOD PAR SMRA, ,GANG ZHIG NYE

NGAR ZHI ZHING BYAMS PA'I THUGS KYIS NI, ,SEMS CAN THAMS CAD
RNAMS LA BRTZE BA GSUNGS PA STE, ,THUGS RJE CHEN PO MNGA' BA DE
LA MCHOD PA NI, ,'TSE BA BYAS NAS BDAG GI LUGS DANG MTSUNGS MA
YIN, ,DE PHYIR GDUNG NI RAB TU SBYIN LAS 'DI RNAMS LA, ,GRAGS PA
DANG NI CHOS KYIS

YANG DAG BGO BA MDZOD, ,DE LTAR GYUR NA KHYED KYIS RTZOD MIN DE
DAG DANG, ,DE DAG GIS KYANG CHOS DANG GRAGS PA 'THOB PAR 'GYUR,
,CHOS LDAN SKYES BU RNAMS KYIS CHOS LAS G-YOS PA NI, ,CHOS LA
'BAD PA LAS KYANG NGED RNAMS KYIS SBYOR NA, ,GANG BDAG RNAMS KYIS
GZHAN DAG CHOS LA SBYOR

BYED PA; ,DE DAG RNAMS KYIS CHOS NI GNAS PA'I CHED DU 'JUG ,DRANG
SRONG DAM PA MCHOG GIS CHOS KYI SBYIN PA NI, ,SBYIN PA THAMS CAD
KYI NI KHYAD PAR 'PHAGS PAR GSUNGS, ,GANG ZHIG LA LAS NOR LA
SBYOR BAR BYED PA STE, ,CHOS KYI SBYIN PA PO NI RNAM PAR BSAGS PA
YIN, ,DE NAS

SNYAN GRAGS DANG NI BDE BA 'DREN PA DANG, ,CHOS KYI TSIG NI DE
LAS NYE BAR THOB NAS NI, ,NGO TSA DANG BCAS PHAN TSUN LTA BA DE
RNAMS KYIS, ,BRE BO'I RIGS MNYAM BRAM ZE LA NI SMRAS PA'O, ,AE MA
MDZA' BO'I DGE LA KHYOD KYIS NGES PA STE, ,YON TAN RNAMS LA BRAM
ZE'I RJES SU MTHUN PAS

@102A *, ,CHAGS; ,LAM GZHAN GYIS NI 'KHRUL BA'I RTA NGAN RNAMS
BZHIN DU, ,GANG GIS LEGS PAR BSNYEN PA'I LAM LA BKOD PAR 'GYUR,
,JI LTAR SMRAS PA DE LTAR DE NI LDAN 'GYUR ZHING, ,BRTZE ZHING
MNYEN PA'I TSIG 'DI 'DZIN PAR RIGS PA STE, ,MDZA' BO'I SKYE BO'I
TSIG LA

SHIN TU 'DAS NAS SU, ,PHYI NAS SDUG BSNGAL NYID DU LHUNG RNAMS
MYA NGAN 'GYUR, ,DE NAS 'GRO BA'I KHAMS RIG GDUNG NI GYAD RNAMS
KYIS, ,DE RNAMS BRGYAD DU GUS PAS YON TAN LAS BGOS SO, ,DE NAS
RANG NYID KYIS NI CHA SHAS BZUNG NAS NI, ,BDUN PO SO SO SO SOR
GZHAN RNAMS LA BYIN TO, ,

GYAD RNAMS DAG GIS MNGON MCHOD SA SKYONG DE RNAMS KYANG, ,DGA'
ZHING DON BYAS RNAMS NI RANG YUL RNAMS SU GSHEGS, ,DE NAS DRANG
SRONG GIS GDUNG DE RNAMS CHO GA BZHIN, ,RANG GRONG RNAMS SU MCHOD
RTEN RAB GNAS RNAMS DE BYAS, ,DE NAS RANG GI YUL DU THUB PA'I
MCHOD RTEN NI, ,BYED 'DOD

BRE BOS SO SOR BGOS PA'I BUM PA BLANGS, ,SOL BA LHAG MA RNAMS
KYANG PI SA LA ZHES PA'I, ,GUS PAS RJES SU RAB LDAN RNAMS KYIS
BSLANGS PAR GYUR, ,DE NAS GDUNG GI SNYING PO CAN GYI SNGON DU
BRGYAD, ,BRAG RI DKAR PO DANG MTSUNGS MCHOD RTEN RNAMS GYUR
ZHING, ,DE YI BUM PAS

BSNYEN PA BRAM ZE'I DGU PA STE, ,SOL BA'I SNYING PO DANG LDAN BCU
PA BYUNG BAR GYUR, ,THUB PA'I MCHOD RTEN SNA TSOGS BA DAN G-YO BA
RNAMS, ,TI SE'I GANGS RI'I RTZE MO DANG MTSUNGS DE RNAMS LA,
,RANG GI SKYE BO DANG BCAS MI SKYONG DE RNAMS DANG, ,SKYE DGU
DANG BCAS BRAM ZE RNAMS KYIS

SA NA MCHOD, ,PHRENG BA MNGON SBYAR RNAMS DANG DRI BZANGS MCHOG
RNAMS DANG, ,PHRENG BA DGE BA RNAMS DANG SIL SNYAN DBYANGS RNAMS
KYIS, ,MCHOD PA DAM PA MI SKYONG DE RNAMS DE RNAMS KYIS, ,RGYAL
BA'I GDUNG NI 'DZIN PA DE RNAMS LA BYAS SO, ,DE NAS DUS SU DGRA
BCOM RNAMS KYI LNGA BRGYA

RNAMS, ,RI BO LNGAS MTSAN GRONG KHYER DU NI YONGS 'DUS NAS, ,SLAR
YANG JI LTA BA BZHIN CHOS NI GNAS PA'I PHYIR, ,THUB PA'I GSUNG NI
RI YI LOGS SU YANG DAG BSDUS, ,GNAS SKABS KUN DU DRANG SRONG CHE
LAS THOS PA NI, ,KUN DGA' BO NYID YIN ZHES NGES PAR GYUR PA YI,
,DGE

@102B SLONG DE RNAMS KYIS NI 'DUS PA MTHUN PA RU, ,GSUNG BAR ZHU
ZHES LUS 'PHAGS THUB PA LA ZHUS SO, ,DE NAS DE DAG RNAMS KYI DBUS
SU DE BZHUGS NAS, ,SMRA BA RNAMS KYI MCHOG GIS JI LTAR GSUNGS
PA'I TSIG ,GANG DU GANG LA GANG GI TSE NA GANG ZHIG DANG, ,'DI
SKAD BDAG

GIS 'DI NI THOS ZHES GSUNGS PAR GYUR, ,DE PHYIR DGRA BCOM RNAMS
KYIS RJES SU BCINGS PA DES, ,THUB PA CHEN PO'I CHOS KYI BSTAN
BCOS GNAS PA STE, ,GANG ZHIG 'BAD PAS YANG DAG RAB TU THOB PA NI,
,MYA NGAN 'DAS SHING 'DA' LA MYA NGAN 'DA' BAR 'GYUR, ,DGRA BO
KHENGS

PA RNAMS KYI MYA NGAN STER BA PO, ,SKYE DGU SDUG BSNGAL RNAMS KYI
MYA NGAN GCOD PA PO, ,ME TOG 'BRAS LDAN MYA NGAN MED LTAR BLTA NA
SDUG ,DUS SU DE GUS SA BDAG MYA NGAN MED PA BYUNG, ,'PHAGS PA MOO
RGYA'I DPAL DES SKYE DGUR PHAN DON DU, ,'JIG RTEN KUN LA MCHOD
RTEN MTSAN MA

BYED DU BCUG ,GTUM PO MYA NGAN MED NYID THOB NAS SA LA NI, ,CHOS
RGYAL MYA NGAN MED NYID LAS DE THOB PAR GYUR, ,MNGON DU BYAS PA'I
MCHOD RTEN BDUN PO DE RNAMS LAS, ,DRANG SRONG DE YI GDUNG RNAMS
MOO RGYA DES BLANGS NAS, ,DPAL LDAN MCHOD RTEN STON KA'I SPRIN
GYI 'OD RNAMS KYI, ,

STONG PHRAG BRGYAD CUR BABS PA DUS SU ZHAG GIS BYAS, ,DGA' BYED
GRONG GNAS MCHOD RTEN BRGYAD PA DANG PO NI, ,DE YI DUS SU GUS
LDAN KLU RNAMS KYIS BSRUNGS TE, ,DE PHYIR GDUNG RNAMS THOB PA MA
YIN RGYAL BO DES, ,DER BYAS PA LA MA DAD RGYA CHEN GYUR PA'O,
,DE'I PHYIR YID KYIS

DGRA BO 'BRAS BU RNAMS LA NI, ,KUN NAS GNAS SHING G-YO BA'I DPAL
NI BSRUNGS NA YANG, ,MI SKYONG DES NI NGUR SMRIG GON PA LAS GZHAN
DU, ,LTA BA RNAM PAR DAG CING 'BRAS BU DANG PO THOB, ,DE LAS
GZHAN DU GZHAN GYIS THUB PA'I MCHOD PA NI, ,GANG GIS BYAS SHING
BYED LA BYED

PAR 'GYUR BA STE, ,DAM PA'I SKYE BOS BSNYEN PA'I 'BRAS BU BLA NA
MED, ,DE YIS THOB CING 'THOB LA 'THOB PAR 'GYUR BA NYID, ,DRANG
SRONG BZHUGS PA LA NI MCHOD PA SBYAR NAS SAM, ,YONGS SU MYA NGAN
'DAS PA'I GDUNG LA PHYAG BYAS NAS, ,YID KYI DANG BA MNYAM NA
'BRAS BU MNYAM PA

@103A *, ,STE; ,SANGS RGYAS YON TAN RNAMS NI MKHAS RNAMS SHES PAR
MDZOD, ,DE PHYIR RTAG TU MCHOG GI CHOS NI MKHYEN PA'O, ,MCHOG TU
MI 'GYUR 'PHO BA MED PA BRNYES LDAN PA, ,BRTZE BA DANG BCAS THUB
PA BLO GROS CHEN PO NI, ,MCHOD 'OS MCHOG LA MCHOD LA DAM

PA 'ONGS PA'O, ,MCHOG TU THUGS RJE DANG LDAN MCHOG GI THUGS
MKHYEN PA, ,GZHAN LA PHAN PHYIR MCHOG TU NGAL BAR BYON PA DE,
,MDZAD PA MKHYEN PA NYID KYIS DAM PA MKHAS RNAMS KYI, ,'DI NA
GTANG RAG MCHOD PA GANG PHYIR 'OS MA YIN, ,SA NA 'CHI DANG RGA BA
DANG MNYAM

'JIGS PA DANG, ,MTHO RIS DAG NA 'PHO BA DANG MNYAM YOD MIN TE,
,'GRO BA'I DE GNYIS MKHYEN NAS GANG ZHIG GNAS PA STE, ,DE PHYIR
MCHOD PAR BYA BA DAM PA SU 'DRA YOD, ,SKYE BA YOD NA BDE BA MIN
PA 'BYUNG BA STE, ,YANG SRID MED LAS SHIN TU BDE BAS BDE BA MED,
,DE

NI BRNYES SHING GANG GIS 'GRO LA BYIN PA STE, ,DE'I PHYIR MCHOD
PAR BYA BA DAM PA SU 'DRA YOD, ,DE LTAR THUB PA'I SKYES MCHOG DE
YI GUS PA YIS, ,MKHAS NYID YON TAN LAS MIN SNYAN DNGAGS NUS PAS
MIN, ,THUB PA'I LUNG GI RJES SU 'BRANGS NAS 'DI BRTZAMS TE, ,SKYE
DGU

RNAMS KYI PHAN DANG BDE BA'I PHYIR GYUR CIG ,YUL SH'A SE TA KA'I
GSER MIG MA'I BU DGE SLONG SLOB DPON SNYAN DNGAGS MKHAN CHEN PO,
,SMRA BA DANG LDAN PA PHYOGS SU RNAM PAR GRAGS PA, BTZUN PA RTA
DBYANGS KYIS MDZAD PA'I, SANGS RGYAS KYI SPYOD PA ZHES BYA BA'I
SNYAN DNGAGS CHEN PO

LAS SKU GDUNG RNAM PAR BGO BA'I LE'U STE NYI SHU RTZA BRGYAD PA
YONGS SU RDZOGS SO,, ,,SA STENGS RGYA MTSO'I MTHAR THUG BSTAN
PA'I BDAG PO MCHOG ,YON TAN MTSUNGS MED PHUL BYUNG DU MA'I GTER
CHEN PO, ,MKHAS PA RNAMS KYI BLA MA SKYE DGU RNAMS KYI DPAL, ,

BLA MA DAM PA CHOS KYI RGYAL PO'I BKA' LUNG GIS, ,'JIG RTEN KUN
NA ZLA BRAL SKYES MCHOG DE NYID KYI, ,PHRIN LAS SGRUB PA SNYE
BA'I THUGS DGONGS RNAM DAG DANG, ,MI RJE LHA SRAS GUNG THANG
RGYAL MO YUM SRAS DANG, ,CHOS LA GCIG TU DKAR BA'I LHA GCIG KUN
DGA' 'BUM, ,MANG YUL

@103B SKYI RONG BZANG MO YON TAN SKYID LA SOGS, ,CHOS LDAN DAM PA
RNAMS KYIS SBYIN BDAG BGYIS PA'I NGOR, ,'PHAGS PA RTA DBYANGS
KYIS MDZAD THUB PA'I MDZAD PA 'DI, ,SA DBANG BZANG PO DANG NI BLO
GROS RGYAL POS BSGYUR, ,'DI BSGYUR BSOD NAMS RGYAL PO GANG DES
PHA MA DANG, ,'GRO

RNAMS LAM GYI RGYAL PO DAM PA 'DIR ZHUGS TE, ,NYES TSOGS TSANG
TSING KUN DANG BDUD BZHI'I RGYAL PO RNAMS, ,BCOM NAS CHOS KYI
